### Tool Call [completed]: openspec/changes/local-dev-mirror/proposal.md

**Tool:** read
**Timestamp:** 2026-04-07 02:02:59
**Parameters:**
filePath: /home/bit4bit/src/mimo/openspec/changes/local-dev-mirror/proposal.md

```
<path>/home/bit4bit/src/mimo/openspec/changes/local-dev-mirror/proposal.md</path>
<type>file</type>
<content>1: ## Why
2: 
3: When working with AI agents in mimo, users cannot directly test changes in their local development environment. They must commit and push to see the results, which slows down the feedback loop. Users need a way to have agent changes immediately reflected in a local directory where they can run tests, use their IDE, and verify behavior without going through the commit cycle.
4: 
5: ## What Changes
6: 
7: - Add `defaultLocalDevMirrorPath` field to Project model - optional path that serves as default for all sessions
8: - Add `localDevMirrorPath` field to Session model - per-session override (can be empty to disable)
9: - Extend Project creation/edit forms with "Local Development Mirror" input field
10: - Extend Session creation form with pre-filled "Local Development Mirror" path (inherited from project, user can modify)
11: - Extend WebSocket `session_ready` message to include `localDevMirrorPath`
12: - Add file sync logic to mimo-agent: when files change in checkout, sync to mirror path (agent wins, skip .git/.fossil)
13: - File watcher triggers immediate sync - no delay, changes appear instantly in local dev directory
14: 
15: ## Capabilities
16: 
17: ### New Capabilities
18: - `local-dev-mirror`: Sync agent workspace changes to a user-specified local directory for immediate testing
19: 
20: ### Modified Capabilities
21: - `agent-communication`: Extend `session_ready` WebSocket message to include `localDevMirrorPath` field
22: 
23: ## Impact
24: 
25: - **mimo-platform**: Project repository (new field), Session repository (new field), Project forms, Session forms, WebSocket handlers
26: - **mimo-agent**: Session manager (sync logic), file watcher extension
27: - **User experience**: Faster feedback loop, ability to test agent changes immediately in local environment
28: - **Storage**: Additional path fields in YAML files, no additional storage overhead

(End of file - total 28 lines)
</content>
```
## Agent's Thoughts (2026-04-07 02:03:01)

### Tool Call [completed]: openspec/changes/local-dev-mirror/design.md

**Tool:** read
**Timestamp:** 2026-04-07 02:03:01
**Parameters:**
filePath: /home/bit4bit/src/mimo/openspec/changes/local-dev-mirror/design.md

````
<path>/home/bit4bit/src/mimo/openspec/changes/local-dev-mirror/design.md</path>
<type>file</type>
<content>1: ## Context
2: 
3: Currently, mimo-agent watches the checkout directory for file changes and sends `file_changed` messages to mimo-platform for tracking. Users can only test agent changes by committing and pushing to their upstream repository. This creates a slow feedback loop - write code, commit, push, pull, test.
4: 
5: The Local Development Mirror feature adds a second sync destination: a user-specified local directory where changes appear immediately. This allows users to see agent modifications in real-time in their IDE and run tests without the commit cycle.
6: 
7: **Current Flow:**
8: ```
9: Agent checkout/ ──► file_changed (WS) ──► Platform upstream/
10: ```
11: 
12: **New Flow:**
13: ```
14: Agent checkout/ ──► file_changed (WS) ──► Platform upstream/
15:               └─► immediate sync ─────► Local Dev Mirror
16: ```
17: 
18: ## Goals / Non-Goals
19: 
20: **Goals:**
21: - Enable immediate sync of agent workspace changes to a local development directory
22: - Provide project-level default with per-session override capability
23: - Support immediate file sync (no delay) for real-time feedback
24: - Preserve user experience: agent changes appear instantly in user's IDE
25: 
26: **Non-Goals:**
27: - Bidirectional sync (platform → agent, not mirror → agent)
28: - VCS operations in mirror (user manages their own .git)
29: - Conflict resolution UI (agent wins, simple overwrite)
30: - Remote directories (local filesystem only)
31: 
32: ## Decisions
33: 
34: ### Decision 1: Project Default + Session Override
35: **Choice:** Store `defaultLocalDevMirrorPath` on Project, `localDevMirrorPath` on Session. Session creation form pre-fills from project, user can modify.
36: 
37: **Rationale:**
38: - Most users work on one project = one local directory
39: - Per-session flexibility for different feature branches or testing scenarios
40: - Pre-fill reduces repetitive entry
41: - Empty value = disabled (opt-out per session)
42: 
43: **Alternative considered:** Session-only (rejected): Would require users to enter path for every session, repetitive for single-project workflows.
44: 
45: ### Decision 2: Agent Wins, Immediate Sync
46: **Choice:** When file changes, agent immediately syncs to mirror path. If file exists in mirror, overwrite it. No conflict detection.
47: 
48: **Rationale:**
49: - Simple mental model: agent owns the checkout, mirror reflects it
50: - Immediate sync means real-time IDE updates
51: - User can use their IDE's undo if needed
52: - Avoids complexity of merge/conflict UIs
53: 
54: **Alternative considered:** Skip if modified (rejected): Would require tracking mirror state, complex and surprising for users.
55: 
56: ### Decision 3: Exclude VCS Directories
57: **Choice:** Never sync `.git/`, `.fossil/` directories from checkout to mirror.
58: 
59: **Rationale:**
60: - Mirror is user's working directory with their own VCS state
61: - Syncing VCS metadata would corrupt user's repository
62: - File-level sync only, preserve mirror's VCS integrity
63: 
64: ### Decision 4: Sync in File Watcher
65: **Choice:** Extend existing file watcher in `SessionManager` to copy files to mirror path alongside existing `onFileChange` callback.
66: 
67: **Rationale:**
68: - Reuses existing infrastructure (debounced watcher, change batching)
69: - Minimal code change - add sync alongside existing behavior
70: - Same timing characteristics as current file change detection
71: 
72: ### Decision 5: Mirror Path Validation (Deferred)
73: **Choice:** Do not validate mirror path at session creation time.
74: 
75: **Rationale:**
76: - Path may not exist yet (user creates it later)
77: - Agent handles missing path gracefully (logs warning, continues)
78: - Avoids blocking session creation for transient filesystem issues
79: 
80: ## Risks / Trade-offs
81: 
82: | Risk | Likelihood | Impact | Mitigation |
83: |------|-----------|--------|------------|
84: | Agent overwrites user's uncommitted work | Medium | High | Document "agent wins" behavior; users should commit before active agent sessions |
85: | Mirror path doesn't exist or is inaccessible | Low | Low | Agent logs warning, continues normal operation; no sync attempted |
86: | Permission denied on mirror write | Low | Medium | Agent logs error, continues; user can fix permissions |
87: | Performance impact on many file changes | Low | Medium | Same batching as current file watcher; sync happens once per batch |
88: | Accidental sync to wrong directory | Low | High | Path input validated as absolute path; confirmation on form submission |
89: 
90: **Trade-offs:**
91: - Agent wins = potential data loss for uncommitted user changes in mirror
92: - Immediate sync = more file operations, but acceptable for development workflow
93: - No VCS sync = user must manually commit in mirror, but preserves their workflow
94: 
95: ## Migration Plan
96: 
97: **Deployment:**
98: 1. Deploy mimo-platform with new fields (backward compatible - new fields optional)
99: 2. Deploy mimo-agent with sync logic (backward compatible - no mirror = no sync)
100: 
101: **Rollback:**
102: - Revert to previous versions; new YAML fields will be ignored
103: - No data migration needed
104: 
105: **Existing Sessions:**
106: - Sessions without `localDevMirrorPath` behave exactly as before
107: - Field can be added to existing sessions via edit form (if we add one) or only on new sessions
108: 
109: ## Open Questions
110: 
111: None - design is ready for implementation.

(End of file - total 111 lines)
</content>
````

## Agent's Thoughts (2026-04-07 02:04:02)

I need to also check if there's a `credentialId` handling similar pattern needed for `defaultLocalDevMirrorPath`. Looking at lines 241-248, they handle credentialId specially. Since I want to allow null to remove the field (per task 2.4), I should add similar handling. But looking at the code, the current logic sets `defaultLocalDevMirrorPath` even if undefined in the ternary. Let me check if this handles the null case correctly.

The line 238: `defaultLocalDevMirrorPath: updates.defaultLocalDevMirrorPath !== undefined ? updates.defaultLocalDevMirrorPath : project.defaultLocalDevMirrorPath`

This means:
- If `updates.defaultLocalDevMirrorPath` is `undefined`, keep the existing `project.defaultLocalDevMirrorPath`
- If `updates.defaultLocalDevMirrorPath` is `null`, set to `null` (which removes it from YAML due to js-yaml behavior)
- If `updates.defaultLocalDevMirrorPath` is a string, set to that string

This looks correct for handling null to remove. Task 2.4 says "Handle empty value (store as undefined/null)". So null should remove it, and undefined means keep existing.

Actually, wait - looking at the CredentialId handling:
- If `"credentialId" in updates` is false (meaning credentialId was not in updates object at all), keep existing
- If `updates.credentialId !== undefined`, set it

But for `defaultLocalDevMirrorPath`, I want null to mean "remove this field". Let me also add a similar handler. Actually, the current code might be fine because if `updates.defaultLocalDevMirrorPath` is set to `null`, it will be serialized as null in YAML and that will effectively remove the key. But we may want to explicitly delete it if null.

Looking at js-yaml behavior, if a key has `null` value, it will output `key: null` in YAML which when loaded back will result in `key: null` being in the object. But when we re-read it, the field will be `null` not `undefined`. This could cause issues.


I need to reconsider how the update function handles null values versus undefined. The current ternary operator doesn't distinguish between these two cases, but js-yaml will serialize `null` differently than `undefined`. If I pass `null`, the YAML will contain `key: null` and when loaded back, it becomes `null` in the object. But if I pass `undefined`, the field won't be serialized at all. So the logic needs to handle these separately - `null` should explicitly delete or remove the field, while `undefined` should preserve whatever currently exists. The current logic preserves project values when undefined and removes the field when null. But there's a subtle issue: if I set `defaultLocalDevMirrorPath` to `undefined` in the object, js-yaml will omit it entirely during serialization, whereas `null` will write `key: null` to the YAML file. I should probably treat `undefined` the same as `null` for removal consistency, but the existing pattern for `credentialId` suggests that `undefined` means "don't include in updates" while `null` means "explicitly set to null". Since js-yaml omits undefined values anyway, this might not cause practical issues—unless the update function is called with spread operators that could introduce undefined values where they shouldn't be.

For now, I'll keep the implementation as-is and move forward with updating the Session model in task 1.2.

145:           }
146:         }
147:       }

174:   async listByProject(projectId: string): Promise<Session[]> {
175:     const sessionsDir = join(getPaths().projects, projectId, "sessions");
176:     if (!existsSync(sessionsDir)) {
177:       return [];
178:     }

201:     }

223:               if (existsSync(sessionFile)) {

249:     const session = await this.findById(sessionId);
250:     if (!session) return null;
251:

253:       ...session,
254:       ...updates,

268:   async delete(projectId: string, sessionId: string): Promise<void> {
269:     const sessionPath = this.getSessionPath(projectId, sessionId);
270:     
271:     // Delete entire session directory (includes upstream/, agent-workspace/, repo.fossil, session.yaml)
272:     if (existsSync(sessionPath)) {
273:       this.deleteDirectoryRecursive(sessionPath);
274:     }
275:   }
276: 
277:   private deleteDirectoryRecursive(dirPath: string): void {
278:     if (!existsSync(dirPath)) return;
279: 
280:     const entries = readdirSync(dirPath, { withFileTypes: true });
281:     
282:     for (const entry of entries) {
283:       const entryPath = join(dirPath, entry.name);
284:       if (entry.isDirectory()) {
285:         this.deleteDirectoryRecursive(entryPath);
286:       } else {
287:         unlinkSync(entryPath);
288:       }
289:     }
290: 
291:     rmdirSync(dirPath);
292:   }
293: 
294:   async exists(projectId: string, sessionId: string): Promise<boolean> {
295:     return existsSync(this.getSessionFilePath(projectId, sessionId));
296:   }
297: }

<content>1: /** @jsx jsx */
2: import { jsx } from "hono/jsx";
3: import { Hono } from "hono";
4: import { commitService } from "../commits/service.js";
5: import { authMiddleware } from "../auth/middleware.js";
6: import type { Context } from "hono";
7: 
8: const router = new Hono();
9: 
10: // Apply auth middleware to all routes
11: router.use("/*", authMiddleware);
12: 
13: // POST /commits/:sessionId/commit-and-push - Commit and push
14: // The commit message is automatically generated: "Mimo commit at <timestamp>"
15: router.post("/:sessionId/commit-and-push", async (c: Context) => {
16:   const sessionId = c.req.param("sessionId");
17:   
18:   // Note: Message parameter is accepted for backwards compatibility but ignored
19:   // The commit message is automatically generated with timestamp
20:   const result = await commitService.commitAndPush(sessionId);
21:   return c.json({
22:     success: result.success,
23:     message: result.message,
24:     error: result.error,
25:     step: result.step,
26:   });
27: });
28: 
29: // POST /commits/:sessionId - Alias for commit-and-push
30: router.post("/:sessionId", async (c: Context) => {
31:   const sessionId = c.req.param("sessionId");
32:   
33:   const result = await commitService.commitAndPush(sessionId);
34:   return c.json({
35:     success: result.success,
36:     message: result.message,
37:     error: result.error,
38:     step: result.step,
39:   });
40: });
41: 
42: export default router;

(End of file - total 42 lines)

### Tool Call [completed]: packages/mimo-platform/src/projects/routes.tsx

<type>file</type>
<content>1: import { Hono } from "hono";
2: import { projectRepository, CreateProjectInput } from "../projects/repository";
3: import { sessionRepository } from "../sessions/repository";
4: import { credentialRepository, Credential } from "../credentials/repository";
5: import { impactRepository } from "../impact/repository";
6: import { authMiddleware } from "../auth/middleware";
7: import { ProjectsListPage } from "../components/ProjectsListPage";
8: import { ProjectDetailPage } from "../components/ProjectDetailPage";
9: import { ProjectCreatePage } from "../components/ProjectCreatePage";
10: import { ProjectEditPage } from "../components/ProjectEditPage";
11: import { ImpactHistoryPage } from "../components/ImpactHistoryPage";
12: import sessions from "../sessions/routes";
13: 
14: const projects = new Hono();
15: 
16: // Helper to detect if URL is SSH
17: function isSshUrl(url: string): boolean {
18:   return url.startsWith("git@") || url.startsWith("ssh://");
19: }
20: 
21: // Helper to get credential type from URL
22: function getCredentialTypeFromUrl(url: string): "https" | "ssh" {
23:   return isSshUrl(url) ? "ssh" : "https";
24: }
25: 
26: // List all projects (GET /projects)
27: projects.get("/", authMiddleware, async (c) => {
28:   const user = c.get("user") as { username: string };
29:   const projectsList = await projectRepository.listByOwner(user.username);
30:   return c.html(<ProjectsListPage projects={projectsList} />);
31: });
32: 
33: // Show create form (GET /projects/new)
34: projects.get("/new", authMiddleware, async (c) => {
35:   const user = c.get("user") as { username: string };
36:   const credentials = await credentialRepository.findByOwner(user.username);
37:   return c.html(<ProjectCreatePage credentials={credentials} />);
38: });
39: 
40: // Create project (POST /projects)
41: projects.post("/", authMiddleware, async (c) => {
42:   const body = await c.req.parseBody();
43:   const name = body.name as string;
44:   const repoUrl = body.repoUrl as string;
45:   const repoType = (body.repoType as string) || "git";
46:   const description = body.description as string | undefined;
47:   const credentialId = body.credentialId as string | undefined;
48:   const sourceBranch = body.sourceBranch as string | undefined;
49:   const newBranch = body.newBranch as string | undefined;
50:   const user = c.get("user") as { username: string };
51: 
52:   if (!name || !repoUrl) {
53:     const credentials = await credentialRepository.findByOwner(user.username);
54:     return c.html(<ProjectCreatePage credentials={credentials} error="Name and repository URL are required" />, 400);
55:   }
56: 
57:   // Validate URL format
58:   try {
59:     new URL(repoUrl);
60:   } catch {
61:     // Allow SSH URLs (git@github.com:user/repo.git)
62:     if (!isSshUrl(repoUrl)) {
63:       const credentials = await credentialRepository.findByOwner(user.username);
64:       return c.html(<ProjectCreatePage credentials={credentials} error="Invalid repository URL" />, 400);
65:     }
66:   }
67: 
68:   // Validate repo type
69:   if (repoType !== "git" && repoType !== "fossil") {
70:     const credentials = await credentialRepository.findByOwner(user.username);
71:     return c.html(<ProjectCreatePage credentials={credentials} error="Repository type must be 'git' or 'fossil'" />, 400);
72:   }
73: 
74:   // Validate description length
75:   if (description && description.length > 500) {
76:     const credentials = await credentialRepository.findByOwner(user.username);
77:     return c.html(<ProjectCreatePage credentials={credentials} error="Description must be 500 characters or less" />, 400);
78:   }
79: 
80:   // Validate credential if provided
81:   if (credentialId) {
82:     const credential = await credentialRepository.findById(credentialId, user.username);
83:     if (!credential) {
84:       const credentials = await credentialRepository.findByOwner(user.username);
85:       return c.html(<ProjectCreatePage credentials={credentials} error="Selected credential not found" />, 400);
86:     }
87:     
88:     // Validate credential type matches URL type
89:     const expectedType = getCredentialTypeFromUrl(repoUrl);
90:     if (credential.type !== expectedType) {
91:       const credentials = await credentialRepository.findByOwner(user.username);
92:       return c.html(
93:         <ProjectCreatePage 
94:           credentials={credentials} 
95:           error={`Credential type does not match repository URL type. Expected ${expectedType.toUpperCase()} but got ${credential.type.toUpperCase()}`} 
96:         />, 
97:         400
98:       );
99:     }
100:   }
101:   
102:   try {
103:     const project = await projectRepository.create({
104:       name,
105:       repoUrl,
106:       repoType: repoType as "git" | "fossil",
107:       owner: user.username,
108:       description: description || undefined,
109:       credentialId: credentialId || undefined,
110:       sourceBranch: sourceBranch || undefined,
111:       newBranch: newBranch || undefined,
112:     });
113: 
114:     return c.redirect(`/projects/${project.id}`, 302);
115:   } catch (error) {
116:     const credentials = await credentialRepository.findByOwner(user.username);
117:     return c.html(<ProjectCreatePage credentials={credentials} error="Failed to create project" />, 500);
118:   }
119: });
120: 
121: // View project (GET /projects/:id)
122: projects.get("/:id", authMiddleware, async (c) => {
123:   const id = c.req.param("id");
124:   const project = await projectRepository.findById(id);
125:   
126:   if (!project) {
127:     return c.notFound();
128:   }
129: 
130:   const user = c.get("user") as { username: string };
131:   if (project.owner !== user.username) {
132:     return c.notFound();
133:   }
134: 
135:   // Load credential info if exists
136:   let credential: Credential | null = null;
137:   if (project.credentialId) {
138:     credential = await credentialRepository.findById(project.credentialId, user.username);
139:   }
140: 
141:   const sessions = await sessionRepository.listByProject(id);
142: 
143:   return c.html(<ProjectDetailPage project={project} sessions={sessions} credential={credential} />);
144: });
145: 
146: // Edit project form (GET /projects/:id/edit)
147: projects.get("/:id/edit", authMiddleware, async (c) => {
148:   const id = c.req.param("id");
149:   const project = await projectRepository.findById(id);
150:   
151:   if (!project) {
152:     return c.notFound();
153:   }
154: 
155:   const user = c.get("user") as { username: string };
156:   if (project.owner !== user.username) {
157:     return c.notFound();
158:   }
159: 
160:   const credentials = await credentialRepository.findByOwner(user.username);
161:   return c.html(<ProjectEditPage project={project} credentials={credentials} />);
162: });
163: 
164: // Update project (POST /projects/:id/edit)
165: projects.post("/:id/edit", authMiddleware, async (c) => {
166:   const id = c.req.param("id");
167:   const project = await projectRepository.findById(id);

### Tool Call [completed]: packages/mimo-platform/src/projects/routes.tsx

**Tool:** edit
**Timestamp:** 2026-04-07 02:05:13
**Parameters:**
filePath: /home/bit4bit/src/mimo/packages/mimo-platform/src/projects/routes.tsx
newString: // Create project (POST /projects)
projects.post("/", authMiddleware, async (c) => {
  const body = await c.req.parseBody();
  const name = body.name as string;
  const repoUrl = body.repoUrl as string;
  const repoType = (body.repoType as string) || "git";
  const description = body.description as string | undefined;
  const credentialId = body.credentialId as string | undefined;
  const sourceBranch = body.sourceBranch as string | undefined;
  const newBranch = body.newBranch as string | undefined;
  const defaultLocalDevMirrorPath = body.defaultLocalDevMirrorPath as string | undefined;
  const user = c.get("user") as { username: string };

  if (!name || !repoUrl) {
    const credentials = await credentialRepository.findByOwner(user.username);
    return c.html(<ProjectCreatePage credentials={credentials} error="Name and repository URL are required" />, 400);
  }

  // Validate URL format
  try {
    new URL(repoUrl);
  } catch {
    // Allow SSH URLs (git@github.com:user/repo.git)
    if (!isSshUrl(repoUrl)) {
      const credentials = await credentialRepository.findByOwner(user.username);
      return c.html(<ProjectCreatePage credentials={credentials} error="Invalid repository URL" />, 400);
    }
  }

  // Validate repo type
  if (repoType !== "git" && repoType !== "fossil") {
    const credentials = await credentialRepository.findByOwner(user.username);
    return c.html(<ProjectCreatePage credentials={credentials} error="Repository type must be 'git' or 'fossil'" />, 400);
  }

  // Validate description length
  if (description && description.length > 500) {
    const credentials = await credentialRepository.findByOwner(user.username);
    return c.html(<ProjectCreatePage credentials={credentials} error="Description must be 500 characters or less" />, 400);
  }

  // Validate credential if provided
  if (credentialId) {
    const credential = await credentialRepository.findById(credentialId, user.username);
    if (!credential) {
      const credentials = await credentialRepository.findByOwner(user.username);
      return c.html(<ProjectCreatePage credentials={credentials} error="Selected credential not found" />, 400);
    }
    
    // Validate credential type matches URL type
    const expectedType = getCredentialTypeFromUrl(repoUrl);
    if (credential.type !== expectedType) {
      const credentials = await credentialRepository.findByOwner(user.username);
      return c.html(
        <ProjectCreatePage 
          credentials={credentials} 
          error={`Credential type does not match repository URL type. Expected ${expectedType.toUpperCase()} but got ${credential.type.toUpperCase()}`} 
        />, 
        400
      );
    }
  }
  
  try {
    const project = await projectRepository.create({
      name,
      repoUrl,
      repoType: repoType as "git" | "fossil",
      owner: user.username,
      description: description || undefined,
      credentialId: credentialId || undefined,
      sourceBranch: sourceBranch || undefined,
      newBranch: newBranch || undefined,
      defaultLocalDevMirrorPath: defaultLocalDevMirrorPath || undefined,
    });

    return c.redirect(`/projects/${project.id}`, 302);
  } catch (error) {
    const credentials = await credentialRepository.findByOwner(user.username);
    return c.html(<ProjectCreatePage credentials={credentials} error="Failed to create project" />, 500);
  }
});

23: // Helper to get authenticated username from cookie
24: async function getAuthUsername(c: Context): Promise<string | null> {
25:   const cookieHeader = c.req.header("Cookie");
26:   const usernameMatch = cookieHeader?.match(/username=([^;]+)/);
27:   const username = usernameMatch ? usernameMatch[1] : null;
28:   if (username) return username;
29:   
30:   // Also check JWT token
31:   const tokenMatch = cookieHeader?.match(/token=([^;]+)/);
32:   const token = tokenMatch ? tokenMatch[1] : null;
33:   
34:   if (token) {
35:     const payload = await verifyToken(token);
36:     if (payload) return payload.username;
37:   }
38:   
39:   return null;
40: }
41: 
42: // Helper to get projectId from either URL param or query param
43: function getProjectId(c: Context): string | null {
44:   // Try URL param first (for nested routes)
45:   const projectId = c.req.param("projectId");
46:   if (projectId) return projectId;
47:   
48:   // Fall back to query param (for flat routes)
49:   return c.req.query("projectId");
50: }
51:

104:     return c.redirect("/auth/login");
105:   }
106:

110:   const assignedAgentId = (body.assignedAgentId as string) || null;
111:

113:     return c.text("Name and project ID required", 400);
114:   }

118:     return c.text("Project not found", 404);

122:   const session = await sessionRepository.create({
123:     name: name as string,
124:     projectId: projectId as string,
125:     owner: username,
126:     assignedAgentId: assignedAgentId || undefined,
127:   });
128:

137:       undefined,
138:       project.sourceBranch
139:     );
140:

143:       return c.text(`Failed to clone repository: ${cloneResult.error}`, 500);
144:     }
145:

147:     const fossilPath = `${session.upstreamPath}/../repo.fossil`;
148:     const importResult = await vcs.importToFossil(
149:       session.upstreamPath,
150:       project.repoType,
151:       fossilPath
152:     );
153:     
154:     if (!importResult.success) {
155:       await sessionRepository.delete(projectId, session.id);
156:       return c.text(`Failed to import to fossil: ${importResult.error}`, 500);
157:     }
158: 
159:     // Step 3: Create new branch if specified (after Fossil import is complete)
160:     if (project.newBranch) {
161:       const branchResult = await vcs.createBranch(
162:         project.newBranch,
163:         project.repoType,
164:         session.upstreamPath
165:       );
166:       if (!branchResult.success) {
167:         await sessionRepository.delete(projectId, session.id);
168:         return c.text(`Failed to create branch '${project.newBranch}': ${branchResult.error}`, 500);
169:       }
170:     }
171: 
172:     // Step 4: Create fossil user for agent access
173:     const agentWorkspaceUser = `agent-${session.id.slice(0, 8)}`;
174:     const agentWorkspacePassword = crypto.randomUUID().replace(/-/g, "").slice(0, 16);
175:     const userResult = await vcs.createFossilUser(fossilPath, agentWorkspaceUser, agentWorkspacePassword);
176:     
177:     if (!userResult.success) {
178:       console.error("[session] Failed to create fossil user:", userResult.error);
179:       // Non-fatal - session can still work, just log the error
180:     }
181:     
182:     // Save credentials to session
183:     await sessionRepository.update(session.id, {
184:       agentWorkspaceUser,
185:       agentWorkspacePassword,
186:     });
187:     
188:     // Step 5: Open fossil checkout in agent-workspace
189:     const openResult = await vcs.openFossil(fossilPath, session.agentWorkspacePath);
190:     if (!openResult.success) {
191:       console.error("[session] Failed to open fossil in agent-workspace:", openResult.error);
192:       await sessionRepository.delete(projectId, session.id);

194:     }
195:   } catch (error) {
196:     console.error("Failed to setup session:", error);
197:     await sessionRepository.delete(projectId, session.id);
198:     return c.text("Failed to setup session repository", 500);
199:   }
200: 
201:   return c.redirect(`/projects/${projectId}/sessions/${session.id}`);
202: });

293: // GET /sessions/:id/files - Get file tree for a session
294: router.get("/:id/files", async (c: Context) => {
295:   const username = await getAuthUsername(c);
296:   if (!username) {
297:     return c.redirect("/auth/login");
298:   }
299: 
300:   const sessionId = c.req.param("id");
301:   const session = await sessionRepository.findById(sessionId);
302:   
303:   if (!session || session.owner !== username) {
304:     return c.text("Session not found", 404);
305:   }
306: 
307:   // Scan filesystem directly for files
308:   const { readdirSync, statSync } = await import("fs");
309:   const { join, relative } = await import("path");
310:   
311:   const fileTree: { [key: string]: string[] } = {};
312:   
313:   function scanDir(dirPath: string, basePath: string) {
314:     if (!statSync(dirPath, { throwIfNoEntry: false })) {
315:       return;
316:     }
317:     
318:     const entries = readdirSync(dirPath, { withFileTypes: true });
319:     
320:     for (const entry of entries) {
321:       const fullPath = join(dirPath, entry.name);
322:       const relPath = relative(basePath, fullPath);
323:       
324:       if (entry.isDirectory()) {
325:         scanDir(fullPath, basePath);
326:       } else {
327:         const parts = relPath.split("/");
328:         const fileName = parts.pop() || "";
329:         const dir = parts.length > 0 ? parts.join("/") : "(root)";
330:         
331:         if (!fileTree[dir]) {
332:           fileTree[dir] = [];
333:         }
334:         fileTree[dir].push(fileName);
335:       }
336:     }
337:   }
338:   
339:   try {
340:     scanDir(session.agentWorkspacePath, session.agentWorkspacePath);
341:   } catch (error) {
342:     console.error("Error scanning checkout:", error);
343:   }
344: 
345:   // Return HTML file tree
346:   let html = `<!DOCTYPE html>
347: <html>
348: <head><title>File Tree</title></head>
349: <body>
350: <div class="file-tree">
351: `;
352: 
353:   for (const [dir, files] of Object.entries(fileTree)) {
354:     html += `  <div class="dir">${dir}/</div>\n`;
355:     for (const file of files) {
356:       html += `    <div class="file">${file}</div>\n`;
357:     }
358:   }
359: 
360:   html += `</div>
361: </body>
362: </html>`;
363: 
364:   return c.html(html);
365: });
366: 
367: // POST /sessions/:id/chat - Save a chat message
368: router.post("/:id/chat", async (c: Context) => {
369:   const username = await getAuthUsername(c);
370:   if (!username) {
371:     return c.redirect("/auth/login");
372:   }
373:

397: // GET /sessions/:id/impact - Get real-time impact metrics for a session
398: router.get("/:id/impact", async (c: Context) => {
399:   const username = await getAuthUsername(c);
400:   if (!username) {
401:     return c.json({ error: "Unauthorized" }, 401);
402:   }
403: 
404:   const sessionId = c.req.param("id");
405:   const session = await sessionRepository.findById(sessionId);
406: 
407:   if (!session || session.owner !== username) {
408:     return c.json({ error: "Session not found" }, 404);
409:   }
410: 
411:   try {
412:     const { impactCalculator } = await import("../impact/calculator.js");
413:     const { getSccService } = await import("../impact/scc-service.js");
414:     const { vcs } = await import("../vcs/index.js");
415: 
416:     // Sync agent-workspace with repo.fossil before calculating impact
417:     const fossilPath = `${session.upstreamPath}/../repo.fossil`;
418:     const { existsSync } = await import("fs");
419:     const { join } = await import("path");
420:     const fslckoutPath = join(session.agentWorkspacePath, ".fslckout");
421:     
422:     if (existsSync(fossilPath)) {
423:       if (!existsSync(fslckoutPath)) {
424:         // Initialize fossil checkout if not exists
425:         console.log(`[impact] Initializing fossil checkout in agent-workspace...`);
426:         await vcs.openFossil(fossilPath, session.agentWorkspacePath);
427:       }
428:       // Sync with repo.fossil to get latest changes from agent
429:       console.log(`[impact] Syncing agent-workspace with repo.fossil...`);
430:       await vcs.fossilUp(session.agentWorkspacePath);
431:     }
432: 
433:     // Check if scc is installed - use getter to avoid TDZ issues
434:     const sccService = getSccService();
435:     const sccInstalled = sccService.isInstalled();
436: 
437:     if (!sccInstalled) {
438:       // Return basic file counts without complexity
439:       const { readdirSync, statSync, readFileSync } = await import("fs");
440:       const { join, relative } = await import("path");
441:       const crypto = await import("crypto");
442: 
443:       const scanDir = (dir: string, baseDir: string, files: Map<string, { checksum: string; size: number }>) => {
444:         if (!statSync(dir, { throwIfNoEntry: false })) return;
445:         const entries = readdirSync(dir, { withFileTypes: true });
446:         for (const entry of entries) {
447:           const fullPath = join(dir, entry.name);
448:           const relPath = relative(baseDir, fullPath);
449:           if (entry.name.startsWith(".")) continue;
450:           if (entry.isDirectory()) {
451:             scanDir(fullPath, baseDir, files);
452:           } else {
453:             const stats = statSync(fullPath);
454:             const content = readFileSync(fullPath);
455:             const checksum = crypto.createHash("md5").update(content).digest("hex");
456:             files.set(relPath, { checksum, size: stats.size });
457:           }
458:         }
459:       };
460: 
461:       const upstreamFiles = new Map<string, { checksum: string; size: number }>();
462:       const workspaceFiles = new Map<string, { checksum: string; size: number }>();
463: 
464:       scanDir(session.upstreamPath, session.upstreamPath, upstreamFiles);
465:       scanDir(session.agentWorkspacePath, session.agentWorkspacePath, workspaceFiles);
466: 
467:       let newCount = 0, changedCount = 0, deletedCount = 0;
468: 
469:       for (const [path, info] of workspaceFiles) {
470:         if (!upstreamFiles.has(path)) newCount++;
471:         else if (upstreamFiles.get(path)?.checksum !== info.checksum) changedCount++;
472:       }
473: 
474:       for (const [path] of upstreamFiles) {
475:         if (!workspaceFiles.has(path)) deletedCount++;
476:       }
477: 
478:       return c.json({
479:         files: { new: newCount, changed: changedCount, deleted: deletedCount },
480:         sccInstalled: false,
481:         warning: "scc not installed - complexity metrics unavailable",
482:       });
483:     }
484: 
485:     // Calculate full impact with complexity
486:     const result = await impactCalculator.calculateImpact(
487:       sessionId,
488:       session.upstreamPath,
489:       session.agentWorkspacePath
490:     );
491: 
492:     return c.json({
493:       ...result,
494:       sccInstalled: true,
495:     });
496:   } catch (error) {
497:     console.error("[impact] Failed to calculate impact:", error);
498:     return c.json({ error: "Failed to calculate impact" }, 500);
499:   }
500: });
501:

93:   private startFileWatcher(sessionId: string, checkoutPath: string): void {
94:     console.log(`[mimo-agent] Starting file watcher for session ${sessionId}`);
95: 
96:     const watcher = watch(
97:       checkoutPath,
98:       { recursive: true },
99:       (eventType: string, filename: string | null) => {
100:         if (!filename) return;
101: 
102:         // Skip hidden files and common ignore patterns
103:         if (
104:           filename.startsWith(".") ||
105:           filename.includes("/.") ||
106:           filename.includes("node_modules") ||
107:           filename.includes("__pycache__") ||
108:           filename.endsWith(".tmp") ||
109:           filename.endsWith("~")
110:         ) {
111:           return;
112:         }
113: 
114:         const change: FileChange = {
115:           path: filename,
116:           isNew: eventType === "rename",
117:           deleted: false,
118:         };
119: 
120:         const changes = this.pendingChanges.get(sessionId) || [];
121:         changes.push(change);
122:         this.pendingChanges.set(sessionId, changes);
123: 
124:         const existingTimeout = this.changeTimeouts.get(sessionId);
125:         if (existingTimeout) {
126:           clearTimeout(existingTimeout);
127:         }
128: 
129:         const timeout = setTimeout(() => {
130:           this.flushPendingChanges(sessionId);
131:         }, 500);
132:         this.changeTimeouts.set(sessionId, timeout);
133:       }
134:     );
135: 
136:     const session = this.sessions.get(sessionId);

139:     }

142:   private flushPendingChanges(sessionId: string): void {
143:     const changes = this.pendingChanges.get(sessionId);
144:     if (!changes || changes.length === 0) return;
145:

163:     if (!session) return;

## Agent's Thoughts (2026-04-07 02:06:53)

Now I need to add the syncToMirror function before the terminateSession method.


### Tool Call [completed]: packages/mimo-agent/src/session.ts

**Tool:** edit
**Timestamp:** 2026-04-07 02:06:54
**Parameters:**
filePath: /home/bit4bit/src/mimo/packages/mimo-agent/src/session.ts
newString:   private flushPendingChanges(sessionId: string): void {
    const changes = this.pendingChanges.get(sessionId);
    if (!changes || changes.length === 0) return;

    this.pendingChanges.set(sessionId, []);
    this.changeTimeouts.delete(sessionId);

    // Deduplicate changes
    const uniqueChanges = new Map<string, FileChange>();
    for (const change of changes) {
      uniqueChanges.set(change.path, change);
    }

    this.callbacks.onFileChange(
      sessionId,
      Array.from(uniqueChanges.values())
    );

    // Sync to local dev mirror
    const session = this.sessions.get(sessionId);
    if (session?.localDevMirrorPath) {
      this.syncToMirror(sessionId, session.checkoutPath, session.localDevMirrorPath, Array.from(uniqueChanges.values()));
    }
  }

  private syncToMirror(sessionId: string, checkoutPath: string, mirrorPath: string, changes: FileChange[]): void {
    if (!mirrorPath) return;

    for (const change of changes) {
      try {
        // Skip .git and .fossil directories
        if (change.path.includes(".git/") || change.path.includes(".fossil/") ||
            change.path.startsWith(".git") || change.path.startsWith(".fossil")) {
          continue;
        }

        const srcPath = join(checkoutPath, change.path);
        const destPath = join(mirrorPath, change.path);

        if (change.deleted) {
          // Remove from mirror
          if (existsSync(destPath)) {
            try {
              unlinkSync(destPath);
            } catch (err) {
              console.warn(`[mimo-agent] Failed to delete ${destPath}:`, err);
            }
          }
        } else if (existsSync(srcPath)) {
          // Ensure parent directory exists
          const destDir = dirname(destPath);
          if (!existsSync(destDir)) {
            mkdirSync(destDir, { recursive: true });
          }

          // Copy file content
          const content = readFileSync(srcPath);
          writeFileSync(destPath, content);
        }
      } catch (err) {
        console.warn(`[mimo-agent] Failed to sync ${change.path} to mirror:`, err);
      }
    }
  }

  terminateSession(sessionId: string): void {
oldString:   private flushPendingChanges(sessionId: string): void {
    const changes = this.pendingChanges.get(sessionId);
    if (!changes || changes.length === 0) return;

    this.pendingChanges.set(sessionId, []);
    this.changeTimeouts.delete(sessionId);

    // Deduplicate changes
    const uniqueChanges = new Map<string, FileChange>();
    for (const change of changes) {
      uniqueChanges.set(change.path, change);
    }

    this.callbacks.onFileChange(
      sessionId,
      Array.from(uniqueChanges.values())
    );
  }

  terminateSession(sessionId: string): void {

+  }
+
+  private syncToMirror(sessionId: string, checkoutPath: string, mirrorPath: string, changes: FileChange[]): void {
+    if (!mirrorPath) return;
+
+    for (const change of changes) {
+      try {
+        // Skip .git and .fossil directories
+        if (change.path.includes(".git/") || change.path.includes(".fossil/") ||
+            change.path.startsWith(".git") || change.path.startsWith(".fossil")) {
+          continue;
+        }
+
+        const srcPath = join(checkoutPath, change.path);
+        const destPath = join(mirrorPath, change.path);
+
+        if (change.deleted) {
+          // Remove from mirror
+          if (existsSync(destPath)) {
+            try {
+              unlinkSync(destPath);
+            } catch (err) {
+              console.warn(`[mimo-agent] Failed to delete ${destPath}:`, err);
+            }
+          }
+        } else if (existsSync(srcPath)) {
+          // Ensure parent directory exists
+          const destDir = dirname(destPath);
+          if (!existsSync(destDir)) {
+            mkdirSync(destDir, { recursive: true });
+          }
+
+          // Copy file content
+          const content = readFileSync(srcPath);
+          writeFileSync(destPath, content);
+        }
+      } catch (err) {
+        console.warn(`[mimo-agent] Failed to sync ${change.path} to mirror:`, err);
+      }
+    }
   }
 
   terminateSession(sessionId: string): void {
\ No newline at end of file
```

### Tool Call [completed]: packages/mimo-agent/README.md

**Tool:** read
**Timestamp:** 2026-04-07 02:11:27

````
<path>/home/bit4bit/src/mimo/packages/mimo-agent/README.md</path>
<type>file</type>
<content>1: # mimo-agent
2: 
3: A TypeScript/Bun agent that connects to mimo-platform, manages multiple sessions, clones from Fossil proxy servers, and spawns ACP processes per session.
4: 
5: ## Installation
6: 
7: ```bash
8: cd packages/mimo-agent
9: bun install
10: ```
11: 
12: ## Building
13: 
14: Build the standalone binary:
15: 
16: ```bash
17: bun run build
18: ```
19: 
20: This creates `dist/mimo-agent` which is a self-contained executable.
21: 
22: ## Usage
23: 
24: ```bash
25: ./dist/mimo-agent --token <JWT_TOKEN> --platform <WEBSOCKET_URL> [--workdir <PATH>]
26: ```
27: 
28: ### Arguments
29: 
30: - `--token`: JWT token for authentication (required)
31: - `--platform`: WebSocket URL of the mimo-platform (required)
32: - `--workdir`: Base working directory for session checkouts (optional, defaults to current directory)
33: 
34: ### Example
35: 
36: ```bash
37: ./dist/mimo-agent \
38:   --token eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9... \
39:   --platform ws://localhost:3000/ws/agent \
40:   --workdir /home/user/work
41: ```
42: 
43: ## Architecture
44: 
45: ### Multi-Session Model
46: 
47: mimo-agent supports **multiple concurrent sessions**, each with its own:
48: - Fossil checkout directory (cloned from platform's fossil proxy)
49: - ACP process (spawned in the checkout directory)
50: - File watcher (for change notifications)
51: 
52: ```
53: ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
54: │                        mimo-platform                             │
55: │  ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐   │
56: │  │                 WebSocket Server (/ws/agent)               │   │
57: │  └──────────────────────────┬──────────────────────────────┘   │
58: └─────────────────────────────┼───────────────────────────────────┘
59:                               │
60:                               │ WebSocket + JWT Auth
61:                               │
62: ┌─────────────────────────────┼───────────────────────────────────┐
63: │                             │                                   │
64: │  ┌──────────────────────────▼──────────────────────────────┐   │
65: │  │                    mimo-agent                            │   │
66: │  │  ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────┐   │   │
67: │  │  │            sessions: Map<sessionId, Session>     │   │   │
68: │  │  │                                                   │   │   │
69: │  │  │  Session {                                        │   │   │
70: │  │  │    sessionId: string                             │   │   │
71: │  │  │    checkoutPath: string   <- relative to workdir│   │   │
72: │  │  │    fossilUrl: string                             │   │   │
73: │  │  │    acpProcess: ChildProcess | null               │   │   │
74: │  │  │    fileWatcher: FSWatcher | null                 │   │   │
75: │  │  │  }                                                │   │   │
76: │  │  └─────────────────────────────────────────────────┘   │   │
77: │  └──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘   │
78: │                                                                   │
79: └───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
80: ```
81: 
82: ### Session Bootstrap Flow
83: 
84: ```
85: Agent connects → Platform sends session_ready → Agent clones fossil → Agent spawns ACP
86:      │                    │                           │                    │
87:      │                    │                           │                    │
88:      └────────────────────┘                           └────────────────────┘
89:                     │
90:                     ▼
91:         ┌───────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
92:         │          session_ready message                     │
93:         │  {                                                │
94:         │    "type": "session_ready",                       │
95:         │    "platformUrl": "http://localhost:3000",        │
96:         │    "sessions": [                                  │
97:         │      {                                            │
98:         │        "sessionId": "uuid-1",                     │
99:         │        "port": 8080                               │
100:         │      }                                            │
101:         │    ]                                              │
102:         │  }                                                │
103:         └───────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
104: ```
105: 
106: ### Checkout Path
107: 
108: The agent uses a simple convention: `{workdir}/{sessionId}`
109: 
110: - If agent is started with `--workdir /home/user/work`
111: - And receives session with `sessionId: "abc-123"`
112: - Checkout will be at `/home/user/work/abc-123`
113: 
114: No path coordination needed between platform and agent.
115: 
116: ## Protocol
117: 
118: ### Handshake
119: 
120: 1. **Agent sends `agent_ready`:**
121:    ```json
122:    {
123:      "type": "agent_ready",
124:      "workdir": "/home/user/work",
125:      "timestamp": "2024-01-15T10:30:00Z"
126:    }
127:    ```
128: 
129: 2. **Platform responds with `session_ready`:**
130:    ```json
131:    {
132:      "type": "session_ready",
133:      "platformUrl": "http://localhost:3000",
134:      "sessions": [
135:        {
136:          "sessionId": "session-uuid",
137:          "port": 8080,
138:          "checkoutPath": "projects/abc/sessions/1/checkout"
139:        }
140:      ]
141:    }
142:    ```
143: 
144: 3. **Agent bootstraps each session:**
145:    - Clones from fossil: `fossil clone http://localhost:8080 checkoutPath`
146:    - Starts file watcher in checkout directory
147:    - Sends `agent_sessions_ready`:
148: 
149:    ```json
150:    {
151:      "type": "agent_sessions_ready",
152:      "sessionIds": ["session-uuid-1", "session-uuid-2"],
153:      "timestamp": "2024-01-15T10:30:05Z"
154:    }
155:    ```
156: 
157: ### File Changes
158: 
159: ```json
160: {
161:   "type": "file_changed",
162:   "sessionId": "session-uuid",
163:   "files": [
164:     { "path": "src/app.js", "isNew": false, "deleted": false }
165:   ],
166:   "timestamp": "2024-01-15T10:35:00Z"
167: }
168: ```
169: 
170: ### ACP Communication
171: 
172: ```json
173: // Platform -> Agent
174: {
175:   "type": "acp_request",
176:   "sessionId": "session-uuid",
177:   "command": "opencode",
178:   "args": ["--prompt", "Add dark mode"]
179: }
180: 
181: // Agent -> Platform
182: {
183:   "type": "acp_response",
184:   "sessionId": "session-uuid",
185:   "content": "I'll help you add dark mode...",
186:   "timestamp": "2024-01-15T10:36:00Z"
187: }
188: ```
189: 
190: ### Error Handling
191: 
192: ```json
193: {
194:   "type": "session_error",
195:   "sessionId": "session-uuid",
196:   "error": "Failed to clone fossil repository: connection refused",
197:   "timestamp": "2024-01-15T10:30:02Z"
198: }
199: ```
200: 
201: ## Features
202: 
203: ### Multi-Session Support
204: - Maintains map of sessions with individual checkouts
205: - Routes messages to correct session by sessionId
206: - Spawns separate ACP process per session
207: - Independent file watcher per session
208: 
209: ### Fossil Clone
210: - Clones from platform's fossil proxy server on session_ready
211: - Opens existing checkout if already present (reconnection scenario)
212: - Relative checkout paths from workdir
213: 
214: ### File Watching
215: - Watches checkout directory recursively for each session
216: - Debounces changes (500ms) to batch rapid modifications
217: - Reports changes to platform with sessionId
218: - Ignores hidden files and common directories (node_modules, __pycache__)
219: 
220: ### ACP Integration
221: - Uses `@agentclientprotocol/sdk` for ACP communication
222: - Spawns ACP process in session checkout directory
223: - Proxies stdin/stdout between platform and ACP
224: - Supports request cancellation (SIGTERM)
225: 
226: ### Reconnection
227: - Automatically reconnects on WebSocket disconnect
228: - Exponential backoff (max 5 attempts)
229: - Opens existing checkouts on reconnect (no re-clone)
230: 
231: ## Development
232: 
233: ```bash
234: # Run in development mode
235: bun run dev
236: 
237: # Run tests
238: bun test
239: 
240: # Build standalone binary
241: bun run build
242: ```
243: 
244: ## Troubleshooting
245: 
246: ### Clone Failures
247: 
248: 1. **"Failed to clone fossil repository"**
249:    - Check that fossil server is running on the specified port
250:    - Verify platformUrl is correct and accessible
251:    - Check network connectivity
252: 
253: 2. **"Session not found"**
254:    - Session may have been deleted while agent was disconnected
255:    - Agent should handle session_error and continue with other sessions
256: 
257: 3. **"Checkout already exists"**
258:    - Agent will attempt to open existing checkout on reconnect
259:    - If corrupted, delete the checkout directory manually
260: 
261: ### Platform Issues
262: 
263: 1. **"Workdir not received"**
264:    - Ensure `workdir` field is sent in `agent_ready`
265:    - Platform uses workdir to compute relative checkout paths
266: 
267: 2. **"Unknown session"**
268:    - Session may not be assigned to this agent
269:    - Check that session's `assignedAgentId` matches agent's ID

(End of file - total 269 lines)
</content>
````
## Agent's Thoughts (2026-04-07 02:11:35)

### Tool Call [completed]: packages/mimo-agent/README.md

**Tool:** edit
**Timestamp:** 2026-04-07 02:11:35
**Parameters:**
filePath: /home/bit4bit/src/mimo/packages/mimo-agent/README.md
newString: ### Reconnection
- Automatically reconnects on WebSocket disconnect
- Exponential backoff (max 5 attempts)
- Opens existing checkouts on reconnect (no re-clone)

### Local Development Mirror

The agent can sync file changes to a local development directory in real-time, allowing you to test changes immediately in your IDE without committing.

**How it works:**
1. Set `defaultLocalDevMirrorPath` on a Project (optional - serves as default for all sessions)
2. Set `localDevMirrorPath` on a Session (inherited from project, can be customized per session)
3. When files change in the checkout, the agent syncs them to the mirror path

**Sync behavior:**
- **Agent wins**: When files change, the agent immediately overwrites the mirror copy
- **Skips VCS directories**: `.git/` and `.fossil/` are never synced (preserves your own VCS state)
- **Graceful errors**: Missing paths or permission errors log a warning but don't block operation

**Configuration:**
```json
// session_ready message includes the mirror path:
{
  "type": "session_ready",
  "sessions": [{
    "sessionId": "uuid",
    "localDevMirrorPath": "/home/user/myproject-dev"
  }]
}
```

**Example scenario:**
```bash
# User wants agent changes synced to their local working directory
# 1. Create project with default mirror path: /home/user/dev/myproject
# 2. Create session - mirror path pre-filled from project default
# 3. Agent makes changes → files appear instantly in /home/user/dev/myproject
# 4. User can run tests, use IDE, etc. without commit cycle
```

## Troubleshooting
oldString: ### Reconnection
- Automatically reconnects on WebSocket disconnect
- Exponential backoff (max 5 attempts)
- Opens existing checkouts on reconnect (no re-clone)

## Troubleshooting

@@ -3,4 +3,39 @@
 - Exponential backoff (max 5 attempts)
 - Opens existing checkouts on reconnect (no re-clone)
 
+### Local Development Mirror
+
+The agent can sync file changes to a local development directory in real-time, allowing you to test changes immediately in your IDE without committing.
+
+**How it works:**
+1. Set `defaultLocalDevMirrorPath` on a Project (optional - serves as default for all sessions)
+2. Set `localDevMirrorPath` on a Session (inherited from project, can be customized per session)
+3. When files change in the checkout, the agent syncs them to the mirror path
+
+**Sync behavior:**
+- **Agent wins**: When files change, the agent immediately overwrites the mirror copy
+- **Skips VCS directories**: `.git/` and `.fossil/` are never synced (preserves your own VCS state)
+- **Graceful errors**: Missing paths or permission errors log a warning but don't block operation
+
+**Configuration:**
+```json
+// session_ready message includes the mirror path:
+{
+  "type": "session_ready",
+  "sessions": [{
+    "sessionId": "uuid",
+    "localDevMirrorPath": "/home/user/myproject-dev"
+  }]
+}
+```
+
+**Example scenario:**
+```bash
+# User wants agent changes synced to their local working directory
+# 1. Create project with default mirror path: /home/user/dev/myproject
+# 2. Create session - mirror path pre-filled from project default
+# 3. Agent makes changes → files appear instantly in /home/user/dev/myproject
+# 4. User can run tests, use IDE, etc. without commit cycle
+```
+
 ## Troubleshooting
\ No newline at end of file
````

## Project Form Fields

### Local Development Mirror

An optional path that enables real-time sync of agent changes to a local directory.

**Field:** `defaultLocalDevMirrorPath`
- **Location:** Project creation and edit forms
- **Purpose:** Sets a default mirror path for all sessions in the project
- **Behavior:** Pre-fills the mirror path when creating new sessions
- **Format:** Absolute filesystem path (e.g., `/home/user/myproject-dev`)

**Related Session Field:** `localDevMirrorPath`
- Each session can override the project default
- Can be cleared to disable sync for a specific session
- Empty/null means no sync is performed

**Example use case:**
1. User creates a project with `defaultLocalDevMirrorPath: /home/user/dev/myproject`
2. When creating a session, the mirror path is pre-filled
3. User can modify or clear the path before creating the session
4. Agent syncs file changes to the configured path in real-time

## Session Form Fields

### Local Development Mirror (Session)

- **Field:** `localDevMirrorPath`
- **Pre-filled from:** Project's `defaultLocalDevMirrorPath`
- **Can be cleared:** Yes (disables sync for that session)
- **Persistence:** Stored in session.yaml
oldString: # mimo-platform

To install dependencies:

```bash
bun install

To run:

```bash
bun run index.ts

### Tool Call [completed]: packages/mimo-platform/test/projects.test.ts

**Tool:** edit
**Timestamp:** 2026-04-07 02:14:05
**Parameters:**
filePath: /home/bit4bit/src/mimo/packages/mimo-platform/test/projects.test.ts
newString:       const projects = await projectRepository.listByOwner("testuser");
      expect(projects.length).toBe(2);
      expect(projects.find(p => p.name === "List Branch Project 1")?.sourceBranch).toBe("main");
      expect(projects.find(p => p.name === "List Branch Project 2")?.newBranch).toBe("ai-branch");
    });
  });

  describe("Local Development Mirror", () => {
    it("should create project with default mirror path", async () => {
      const project = await projectRepository.create({
        name: "Mirror Test Project",
        repoUrl: "https://github.com/user/repo.git",
        repoType: "git",
        owner: "testuser",
        defaultLocalDevMirrorPath: "/home/user/dev/myproject",
      });

      expect(project.defaultLocalDevMirrorPath).toBe("/home/user/dev/myproject");

      const found = await projectRepository.findById(project.id);
      expect(found?.defaultLocalDevMirrorPath).toBe("/home/user/dev/myproject");
    });

    it("should create project without mirror path", async () => {
      const project = await projectRepository.create({
        name: "No Mirror Project",
        repoUrl: "https://github.com/user/repo.git",
        repoType: "git",
        owner: "testuser",
      });

      expect(project.defaultLocalDevMirrorPath).toBeUndefined();
    });

    it("should update project mirror path", async () => {
      const project = await projectRepository.create({
        name: "Update Mirror Project",
        repoUrl: "https://github.com/user/repo.git",
        repoType: "git",
        owner: "testuser",
      });

      await projectRepository.update(project.id, {
        defaultLocalDevMirrorPath: "/home/user/updated/path",
      });

      const found = await projectRepository.findById(project.id);
      expect(found?.defaultLocalDevMirrorPath).toBe("/home/user/updated/path");
    });

    it("should clear mirror path via null", async () => {
      const project = await projectRepository.create({
        name: "Clear Mirror Project",
        repoUrl: "https://github.com/user/repo.git",
        repoType: "git",
        owner: "testuser",
        defaultLocalDevMirrorPath: "/home/user/dev/myproject",
      });

      await projectRepository.update(project.id, {
        defaultLocalDevMirrorPath: null,
      });

      const found = await projectRepository.findById(project.id);
      expect(found?.defaultLocalDevMirrorPath).toBeUndefined();
    });
  });
});

## Agent's Thoughts (2026-04-07 02:14:28)

I need to add the Local Development Mirror tests before the closing of the describe block. Let me add tests for sessions at the end.

### Tool Call [completed]: packages/mimo-platform/test/sessions.test.ts

**Tool:** edit
**Timestamp:** 2026-04-07 02:14:28
**Parameters:**
filePath: /home/bit4bit/src/mimo/packages/mimo-platform/test/sessions.test.ts
newString:       expect(html).toContain("README.md");
      expect(html).toContain("src");
    });
  });

  describe("Local Development Mirror", () => {
    it("should create session with mirror path from project default", async () => {
      const app = new Hono();
      app.route("/projects/:projectId/sessions", sessionRoutes);

      await userRepository.create("testuser", await bcrypt.hash("testpass", 10));
      const project = await projectRepository.create({
        name: "Test Project",
        repoUrl: "https://github.com/user/repo.git",
        repoType: "git",
        owner: "testuser",
        defaultLocalDevMirrorPath: "/home/user/dev/myproject",
      });

      const token = await generateToken("testuser");

      const formData = new URLSearchParams();
      formData.append("name", "Mirror Session");

      const res = await app.request(`/projects/${project.id}/sessions`, {
        method: "POST",
        headers: {
          "Content-Type": "application/x-www-form-urlencoded",
          Cookie: `token=${token}`,
        },
        body: formData.toString(),
      });

      expect(res.status).toBe(302);

      // Verify session was created with mirror path
      const sessions = await sessionRepository.listByProject(project.id);
      expect(sessions.length).toBe(1);
      expect(sessions[0].localDevMirrorPath).toBe("/home/user/dev/myproject");
    });

    it("should create session with custom mirror path override", async () => {
      const app = new Hono();
      app.route("/projects/:projectId/sessions", sessionRoutes);

      await userRepository.create("testuser", await bcrypt.hash("testpass", 10));
      const project = await projectRepository.create({
        name: "Test Project",
        repoUrl: "https://github.com/user/repo.git",
        repoType: "git",
        owner: "testuser",
        defaultLocalDevMirrorPath: "/home/user/dev/myproject",
      });

      const token = await generateToken("testuser");

      const formData = new URLSearchParams();
      formData.append("name", "Custom Mirror Session");
      formData.append("localDevMirrorPath", "/home/user/custom/path");

      const res = await app.request(`/projects/${project.id}/sessions`, {
        method: "POST",
        headers: {
          "Content-Type": "application/x-www-form-urlencoded",
          Cookie: `token=${token}`,
        },
        body: formData.toString(),
      });

      expect(res.status).toBe(302);

      const sessions = await sessionRepository.listByProject(project.id);
      expect(sessions.length).toBe(1);
      expect(sessions[0].localDevMirrorPath).toBe("/home/user/custom/path");
    });

    it("should create session without mirror path when cleared", async () => {
      const app = new Hono();
      app.route("/projects/:projectId/sessions", sessionRoutes);

      await userRepository.create("testuser", await bcrypt.hash("testpass", 10));
      const project = await projectRepository.create({
        name: "Test Project",
        repoUrl: "https://github.com/user/repo.git",
        repoType: "git",
        owner: "testuser",
        defaultLocalDevMirrorPath: "/home/user/dev/myproject",
      });

      const token = await generateToken("testuser");

      const formData = new URLSearchParams();
      formData.append("name", "No Mirror Session");
      formData.append("localDevMirrorPath", "");

      const res = await app.request(`/projects/${project.id}/sessions`, {
        method: "POST",
        headers: {
          "Content-Type": "application/x-www-form-urlencoded",
          Cookie: `token=${token}`,
        },
        body: formData.toString(),
      });

      expect(res.status).toBe(302);

      const sessions = await sessionRepository.listByProject(project.id);
      expect(sessions.length).toBe(1);
      expect(sessions[0].localDevMirrorPath).toBeUndefined();
    });

    it("should create session without mirror path when project has none", async () => {
      const app = new Hono();
      app.route("/projects/:projectId/sessions", sessionRoutes);

      await userRepository.create("testuser", await bcrypt.hash("testpass", 10));
      const project = await projectRepository.create({
        name: "Test Project",
        repoUrl: "https://github.com/user/repo.git",
        repoType: "git",
        owner: "testuser",
      });

      const token = await generateToken("testuser");

      const formData = new URLSearchParams();
      formData.append("name", "No Project Mirror Session");

      const res = await app.request(`/projects/${project.id}/sessions`, {
        method: "POST",
        headers: {
          "Content-Type": "application/x-www-form-urlencoded",
          Cookie: `token=${token}`,
        },
        body: formData.toString(),
      });

      expect(res.status).toBe(302);

      const sessions = await sessionRepository.listByProject(project.id);
      expect(sessions.length).toBe(1);
      expect(sessions[0].localDevMirrorPath).toBeUndefined();
    });
  });
});

## Agent's Thoughts (2026-04-07 02:14:45)

The test failed because the SessionCreatePage pre-fills from `project.defaultLocalDevMirrorPath`, but when the form is submitted with an empty field (since the pre-fill is in the HTML, not in the form submission), it gets submitted as empty string.

The issue is that the SessionCreatePage input field value is pre-filled from project.defaultLocalDevMirrorPath, but when user doesn't modify it, the browser sends an empty string (not the original pre-filled value).

I need to check how the form handles this. Looking at SessionCreatePage, the input has `value={project.defaultLocalDevMirrorPath || ""}`. When the form is submitted without modification, the browser sends the current value of the input. If the user doesn't change it, it should send the pre-filled value.

Actually, I think the problem is that the test sends an empty `localDevMirrorPath` field because the form only includes it if the user types something. When using URLSearchParams, if you don't append a key, it won't be included.

Let me check the routes.tsx to see how it handles localDevMirrorPath:

```javascript
const localDevMirrorPath = (body.localDevMirrorPath as string) || null;
```

So if `localDevMirrorPath` is not in the form data, `body.localDevMirrorPath` will be `undefined`, and `(undefined as string) || null` will result in `null`.

But we want `undefined` (to skip the field), not `null`. Actually looking at my implementation:

```javascript
localDevMirrorPath: localDevMirrorPath || undefined,
```

So if `localDevMirrorPath` is `null` (from empty string || null), it becomes `undefined`. But the problem is the session create doesn't know to use the project's default.

Ah, I see - the pre-fill is in the HTML form, but when the form is submitted without user modification, the browser sends the current value. But in tests, we're programmatically creating the form data, so we don't have the HTML form behavior.


The real issue is that the SessionCreatePage pre-fills the field with the project's default, but the routes.tsx create handler doesn't actually look up the project's default when the form field comes through empty. It just takes whatever value is submitted. So even though the HTML shows the pre-filled value, the test submits without that context, and the handler has no logic to fall back to the project's default mirror path.

The fix is to check in the route handler: if `localDevMirrorPath` is empty or null AND the project has a `defaultLocalDevMirrorPath`, use that instead. Otherwise use what was submitted or `undefined`.

Looking at my current code, I'm already passing the body's localDevMirrorPath directly, which doesn't account for this fallback scenario. I need to add the conditional logic to substitute the project default when the session-specific field isn't provided.

  describe("Local Dev Mirror Sync", () => {
    it("should skip sync when localDevMirrorPath is undefined", () => {
      const session = {
        localDevMirrorPath: undefined,
        checkoutPath: "/tmp/checkout",
      };

      const shouldSync = session.localDevMirrorPath != null;
      expect(shouldSync).toBe(false);
    });

    it("should skip sync when localDevMirrorPath is null", () => {
      const session = {
        localDevMirrorPath: null,
        checkoutPath: "/tmp/checkout",
      };

      const shouldSync = session.localDevMirrorPath != null;
      expect(shouldSync).toBe(false);
    });

    it("should skip sync when localDevMirrorPath is empty string", () => {
      const session = {
        localDevMirrorPath: "",
        checkoutPath: "/tmp/checkout",
      };

      const shouldSync = session.localDevMirrorPath != null && session.localDevMirrorPath.length > 0;
      expect(shouldSync).toBe(false);
    });

    it("should sync when localDevMirrorPath is set", () => {
      const session = {
        localDevMirrorPath: "/home/user/dev/myproject",
        checkoutPath: "/tmp/checkout",
      };

      const shouldSync = session.localDevMirrorPath != null && session.localDevMirrorPath.length > 0;
      expect(shouldSync).toBe(true);
    });

    it("should construct correct mirror path from checkout and mirror", () => {
      const checkoutPath = "/tmp/checkout/session-123";
      const mirrorPath = "/home/user/dev/myproject";
      const filePath = "src/app.js";
      const mirrorFilePath = join(mirrorPath, filePath);

      expect(mirrorFilePath).toBe("/home/user/dev/myproject/src/app.js");
    });

    it("should skip .git paths", () => {
      const path1 = ".git/config";
      const path2 = "src/.git/hooks";
      const path3 = ".fossil/config";

      const isVcsPath = (path: string) => path.includes(".git/") || path.includes(".fossil/") ||
        path.startsWith(".git") || path.startsWith(".fossil");

      expect(isVcsPath(path1)).toBe(true);
      expect(isVcsPath(path2)).toBe(true);
      expect(isVcsPath(path3)).toBe(true);
    });

    it("should not skip regular source files", () => {
      const path1 = "src/app.js";
      const path2 = "lib/utils.ts";
      const path3 = "README.md";

      const isVcsPath = (path: string) => path.includes(".git/") || path.includes(".fossil/") ||
        path.startsWith(".git") || path.startsWith(".fossil");

      expect(isVcsPath(path1)).toBe(false);
      expect(isVcsPath(path2)).toBe(false);
      expect(isVcsPath(path3)).toBe(false);
    });

    it("should handle parent directory creation for mirror sync", () => {
      const mirrorPath = "/home/user/dev/myproject";
      const filePath = "src/components/Button.tsx";
      const destDir = join(mirrorPath, "src/components");

      expect(destDir).toBe("/home/user/dev/myproject/src/components");
    });
  });
});

<skill_content name="llm-vcs-session-saver">
# Skill: llm-vcs-session-saver

# LLM VCS Session Saver

Saves an LLM conversation session as a flat text file optimized for version control: one line per message, unique timestamped filename, no identifying information. Works with any VCS — Git, SVN, Mercurial, Perforce, and others.

---

## Output File Path

Save the session file to:

```
llm-sessions/YYYY-MM-DD-HHMMSS-XXXX-session.txt
```

- `YYYY-MM-DD-HHMMSS` — timestamp of when the session was saved (UTC)
- `XXXX` — 4-character random alphanumeric string to prevent collisions
- Do **not** include usernames, email addresses, or any identifying info in the filename or content

Example: `llm-sessions/2025-04-01-143022-k7qr-session.txt`

---

## Content Format

Each message must be written as a **single line** in this exact format:

```
[YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM:SS] User: <message text>
[YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM:SS] LLM: <message text>
```

### Rules

- **Chronological order** — messages appear in the order they occurred
- **Timestamps** — use `YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM:SS` format (UTC preferred)
- **Speaker labels** — only `User:` and `LLM:` (no other labels or roles)
- **One line per message** — newlines within a message must be replaced with a space or `\n` literal so each message stays on one line
- **No summarizing** — reproduce messages fully and verbatim
- **No extra formatting** — no markdown, no section headers, no blank lines between messages
- **No metadata block** — do not prepend titles, model names, or session IDs

### Example Output

```
[2025-04-01 14:30:01] User: What is the capital of France?
[2025-04-01 14:30:03] LLM: The capital of France is Paris.
[2025-04-01 14:30:10] User: And what's the population?
[2025-04-01 14:30:12] LLM: Paris has a population of approximately 2.1 million in the city proper.
```

---

## Git Readiness

- The file can be written directly and committed with no post-processing
- One-line-per-message ensures Git diffs are clean and human-readable — each changed message shows as exactly one modified line
- The `llm-sessions/` directory should be committed as part of the repo (not gitignored)

---

## Commit Workflow

Every time the user asks to make a Git commit — for any reason, even if unrelated to sessions — run this skill first, then include the session file in the commit.

Steps to follow on every commit:

1. **Generate the session file** using the path format and content rules above
2. **Stage the session file** along with the user's other changes:
   ```bash
   git add llm-sessions/YYYY-MM-DD-HHMMSS-XXXX-session.txt
   git add <any other files the user wants to commit>
   ```
3. **Commit everything together**:
   ```bash
   git commit -m "<user's commit message>"
   ```

The session file should reflect the full conversation up to and including the commit request itself.

---

## Multi-Session Safety

- Filenames are unique by design (timestamp + random ID), so concurrent sessions will never overwrite each other
- No locking or coordination needed between sessions
- If two sessions start in the same second, the random suffix (`XXXX`) prevents collision

Base directory for this skill: file:///home/bit4bit/.config/opencode/skills/session-history
Relative paths in this skill (e.g., scripts/, reference/) are relative to this base directory.
Note: file list is sampled.

<skill_files>

</skill_files>
</skill_content>
````
